======== Scenario: col_tadpolingcentre ========
Session Sequence: AD_MemoryImprint_003_Mindflayer -> AD_MemoryImprint_004_Mindflayer -> AD_MemoryImprint_006_Zevlor -> Pods -> PAD_BrinePool_Tadpole -> AD_MemoryImprint_005_Mindflayer -> AD_MemoryImprint_007_Mindflayer -> DaisyAD_BrinePool -> AD_MemoryImprint_009_Empty -> PAD_MizoraPodComment -> AD_MemoryImprint_008_Yeva -> AD_Minthara_EnteredTadpolingCenter -> AD_MemoryImprint_001_Mindflayer -> AD_MemoryImprint_010_Empty_Ravengard -> AD_Zevlor_Combat

Narrator: *The device releases a stream of fragmented memories and emotions - all that remains of the pod inhabitant's former self.*
Narrator: *Desperation... pain... terror. Cultists raided his village - he was the sole survivor.*

----- Session: AD_MemoryImprint_004_Mindflayer -----

----- Session: AD_MemoryImprint_006_Zevlor -----
Synopsis: AD for Zevlor's memory imprint in the Tadpoling Centre, showing a memory from before he was imprisoned here.

Narrator: *You remember the shattered windows of Elturel's High Cathedral, the burning black sky of Avernus beyond.*
Narrator: *In its horror, the Blood War unites you. Tiefling, dwarf and elf alike huddle behind the shields of your paladin order, waiting for salvation. But when it comes... disunity.*
Narrator: *The returned city casts your people out, the devils who dragged them down to hell. In the end, it is not your paladin oath that is broken: it is your faith itself.*

----- Session: Pods -----
Synopsis: Interacting with the mind flayer device in the Tadpoling Centre that controls the pods inside. You get to choose whether to free or purge the occupants of the pods - mind flayers and innocents alike.

Narrator: *You connect to the device, and gain control of the pods - and the fate of their occupants.*
Narrator: *The device is open to your tadpole's command - to your authority.*

Narrator: *Screams. Psychic agony. Terror. Then... nothing.*

======== Scenario: col_kethericshowdown ========
Session Sequence: ChosenThree -> DaisyAD_ElderBrain -> DaisyAD_EntranceDoor -> PAD_NightsongCaged -> AD_Phase3Transition -> KethericIntro -> KethericDefeated -> KethericApostle -> PAD_AfterCombatComment -> AD_KethericInvulnerable -> DaisyAD_GrabNetherstone
----- Session: ChosenThree -----
Synopsis: Upon entering the Ketheric boss chamber on the lower floor of the Colony, the party will see a cinematic of the Chosen Three gearing up to continue on to the next stage of their master plan. Ketheric, Orin and Gortash will be discussing the next steps and the tension caused by the player's actions. Ketheric tadpoles Duke Ravengard and we lay eyes upon the Elder Brain in the flesh. Orin and Gortash depart with the Duke and the Elder Brain in a nearby Nautiloid to march onto Baldur's Gate. We see the Nautiloid appear above Moonrise Towers and cue the armies of the Absolute to start marching. Ketheric stays behind to deal with some local issues.

Lord Enver Gortash: You said it was under control. || [context] CinematicNodeContext: Ketheric and Gortash stand by the chamber's centre, squaring off. Nearby, Orin completes the circle, sitting at her leisure on Ravengard by the brine pool.
Ketheric Thorm: It isn't you I answer to, Gortash.
Lord Enver Gortash: Oh, the General voice. Is this where we salute?
Orin: Salute, yes, with cleavers through his blood-starved flesh. How it crawls with failure like flies on lick-wet carrion.
Ketheric Thorm: You forget yourself, Orin. I have played my part.
Lord Enver Gortash: You've built an army for our masters, true enough. But what of the Astral Prism?
Lord Enver Gortash: A rogue True Soul, flaunting it under your nose all this time. And you ran from them.
Ketheric Thorm: Sure that they would follow, and deliver it into my hands here. If you would cease these distractions -

----- Session: AD_Phase3Transition -----
Synopsis: This AD plays during the Ketheric Showdown in the lower Colony, when the third phase of the fight starts, this will play only once on Ketheric when his turn starts. Ketheric, in his Apostle of Myrkul form, calls upon the Necromites to sacrifice themselves to heal him.

: UNLIFE TO MY LIFE - SUSTAIN ME, SLAVES.

----- Session: KethericIntro -----
Synopsis: This dialog plays at the start of the Ketheric boss fight in the Colony. There are numerous permutations here: Nightsong being dead or alive, freed from her soul cage (through stealth before being spotted); Isobel being absent or tadpoled or tadpoled and killed (in the boss chamber) before entering the dialog; Jaheira being present here (and spotted) or being absent.

Ketheric Thorm: There you are. As predicted. What is it, I wonder, that draws one toward death like a moth to light?
Ketheric Thorm: You could have run away. Absconded with the Prism - the one thing that could prevent me from fulfilling my destiny.
Ketheric Thorm: But the lure of one's destiny is irresistible, isn't it?
Ketheric Thorm: Perhaps you hoped to learn your place in history before you are erased from it. A bright flash of clarity before the snuffing-out.
Player: Why is the Prism so important to you?
Ketheric Thorm: The very fact of your being attests to its power - despite your infection, you resisted the brain, here in the heart of its domain.
Ketheric Thorm: What good is an army of thralls if they do not obey their master?
Ketheric Thorm: Let us speak plainly.
Ketheric Thorm: My Lord Myrkul gave me the one thing I desired - the one thing that no other god could grant me.
Ketheric Thorm: My daughter's life returned. Her heart beating once more.
Ketheric Thorm: For that, he asked that I serve as his Chosen, join Orin and Gortash to grow the cult of the Absolute, and then... take control of it.
Ketheric Thorm: He's never had a more devoted follower.
Ketheric Thorm: I have fought great wars before, in the service of other gods, and other powers. But for Myrkul, I would condemn all of Faerûn to death.
Ketheric Thorm: You are all that stands between me and my destiny - and you have brought the Prism here.
Ketheric Thorm: I will kill you now. And then I will raise you as my servant. || [context] NodeContext: Cold, merciless ire.
Player: Enough talk. Let's finish this.
Ketheric Thorm: With pleasure.

: True

----- Session: AD_Butcher_Idle -----
Synopsis: Sequential, repeated AD for Chop, the Colony butcher. He will say a line every few seconds while in his idle behaviour. Chop is generally enjoying his job, but something deep beneath his enthralled exterior realizes the horror of his reality. Some of these lines could be considered a little bit song-like - Chop would be humming to himself while working.

Chop: Pretty faces go chop... faces? No - no faces, only meat. Never think, never stop. Only chop. Chop. CHOP. || [context] NodeContext: Brief note of lucidity on '...faces?' as he seems momentarily aware of his condition - then shakes it off and returns to his work rhythm a little more forcefully.

Us: They are not kind to Us here. We are different, they say. Aberrant. || [context] NodeContext: Pleading
Us: They wish to repurpose Us - destroy what they cannot fix. Please, help Us escape harm! || [context] NodeContext: Pleading

Us: Oh, thank you, thank you! You are a good friend - no, more. Rescuer. || [context] NodeContext: Relieved/grateful

======== Scenario: sce_cursedfist ========
Session Sequence: 
----- Session:  -----
Synopsis: This covers arts three states 1) Thaniel is dead, which means the curse cannot be lifted [he is heartbroken and grieving] 2) the curse quest is in progress, and Thaniel hasn't been saved yet [he's worried for thaniel and frantic] and 3) curse has been lifted and Thaniel is safe [Art is grateful and contemplative, but also a little reserved - he knows he's going to die soon]

Art Cullagh: When Duke Eltan formed the Flaming Fist, he sought out people of courage and honour to fill its ranks.
Art Cullagh: You saved Thaniel, lifted the curse, and killed an immortal.
Art Cullagh: It's safe to say, you'd have been recruited in an instant.
Player: Thank you - it would have been an honour to serve under Duke Eltan.
Art Cullagh: Of course, I have no idea what life is like under Duke Ravengard's rule.
Art Cullagh: But I've seen the respect he inspires in the Flaming Fist - and that tells me all I need about him as a leader.
Art Cullagh: I hope you can save Duke Ravengard - for the good of Baldur's Gate.
Player: Come with me - I could use a Flaming Fist by my side.
Art Cullagh: Thank you, but look at me - I am a relic: a glimpse of history barely strong enough to stand on his own two feet.
Art Cullagh: Besides - Thaniel should have someone here when he wakes up. It's the least I can do.
Player: Then I wish you luck. Thank you for your help. || [approval] ['Gale 1', 'Wyll 1', 'Karlach 1', 'Halsin 1']
Art Cullagh: You too, my friend. Thank you - from Thaniel and I.

======== Scenario: sce_isobelnightsongreunion ========
Session Sequence: 
----- Session:  -----
Synopsis: If Isobel and Nightsong survive Act 2 they will be having a heartfelt reunion during the Epilogue

Isobel: Ah! It's you, isn't it? You're the talk of this place, you know. I'm Isobel, and this is -
Nightsong: Ho! But we have met. This is the soldier that freed me most valiantly from the Shadowfell.
Nightsong: They watched my boot crush the very brain of villainy - and fought well against your changèd father. || [context] NodeContext: old timey change-ed
Isobel: May he rest in peace at last, now that he's dead. || [context] NodeContext: About her father. Tinged with sadness but not too sad. She's about to thank the player warmly.
Isobel: I have more to thank you for than I knew. And we have much to discuss. Perhaps we could join you in your camp later?
Player: Firstly, allow me to apologise to Dame Aylin. My actions were strategy - not personal. || [approval] ['Karlach 1', 'Gale 1', 'Wyll 1', 'Astarion 1', 'Shadowheart 1', "Lae'zel 1", 'Minthara 1']
Nightsong: My forgiveness will be the same. I'd be a fool to turn down a powerful ally - especially one who has earned the trust of fair Isobel.
Nightsong: But Dame Aylin's life is neverending. And she does not forget. Now - I believe Isobel asked a question of you. We will meet you in your camp - is it agreed?
Player: It's a little crowded already.
Isobel: We'll make our visit brief. Cleric's honour.

======== Scenario: moo_flyingghoul ========

----- Session:  -----
Synopsis: The player encounters a pack of winged ghouls on Moonrise's upper exterior. They are disgusting undead who are eternally starving for dead and rotting flesh. Though intelligent, they can be near feral in their need to feed.In this case, the player meets a still-intelligent one with two less-bright comrades. The leader challenges the player, saying the cult has promised them plenty of meat but they've received none. Instead, the corpses are dropped below the tower (unbeknownst to them, to be fed to the Elder Brain or used in the Necromancer's experiments)

Winged Horror: Foot-flesh! || [context] NodeContext: Feral, starving - catching player's scent

----- Session: Drow -----
Synopsis: Minthara is being psychically tortured in the Moonrise Tower dungeon, having been sent there for failing in her mission to capture the weapon the Absolute was seeking (the Orpheus artefact).Two drow guards are torturing her, but they do not lay a finger on her. Instead, they have stripped away her psychic defenses and are using mind-melds to destroy her from the inside.The player can free her by killing the guards, or by mind-melding with Minthara and pulling her out of the despair. If she is freed from the mind-meld while the guards are alive, she kills them.The player can also destroy Minthara completely, by telepathically lobotomising her inside her own mind.

Nightwarden Minthara: I expected to be greeted as a hero - but the wretches imprisoned me, and tried to tear my mind apart.
Nightwarden Minthara: I didn't think anyone would come for me.
Player: We need to get out of here.
Nightwarden Minthara: Agreed.

Questioner Sumera: A whole city in service of the Absolute - it will be glorious.
Questioner Jasin: And so many minds for us to break.

======== Scenario: scl_servantoftheraven ========
Session Sequence: Raven_AD_GoBack -> Raven -> Memories -> Madeline_SwD -> AD_Idle -> AD_TakingTurn_003_Combat
----- Session: Raven_AD_GoBack -----
Synopsis: A brief AD ment to remind the player to go back to shadar kai.

Raven: You found the ledger? Guess you're not so useless. Get back to master, on the double! || [context] NodeContext: condescending and arrogant

----- Session: Raven -----
Synopsis: You talk to a Raven in the shadow-cursed lands. Part of the Servant of the Raven booster.

Narrator: *The raven looks at you with cold, dead eyes.*
Narrator: *The raven stares at you.*
Player: Examine the raven.
: True
Narrator: *There is a malevolence in this bird - rooted deep. It would not be wise to touch it.*

----- Session: Memories -----
Synopsis: The player has delivered Madeline's ledger to He Who Was. The shadar-kai uses the book to channel her spirit. Player can punish her, making her stab herself the way her friends died, verbally admonish her, or forgive her.

He Who Was: The air stirs in trepidation - you have the ledger. || [context] NodeContext: Col, calculated tone
Player: Here - take it.
He Who Was: We have it - her lies, her guilt. Madeline reported her friends to a Dark Justiciar and fled when they were butchered. || [context] NodeContext: a touch of excitement begins to creep into the usually cold tone. Cruel smile.
He Who Was: Well, she flees no more. I will be the conduit for Madeline's spirit. I will force her to face trial. || [context] NodeContext: a touch of excitement begins to creep into the usually cold tone. Cruel smile.
He Who Was: And you will be the judge. Make her beg, make her suffer. || [context] NodeContext: a touch of excitement begins to creep into the usually cold tone. Cruel smile.
Player: When punishment is needed, my hand will not shy from the blade.
He Who Was: The raven was right, we were fated to meet. Break her, my friend - most thoroughly. || [context] NodeContext: pleased the player agrees with him, thinks they are of one mind and both enjoy cruelty
He Who Was: What's this? The ledger is gone - how curious. Without it, the ceremony is an impossibility. || [context] NodeContext: Patting down his 'pockets' like he's looking for something. Irritated. 'how curious' glares at player with a clear accusation (the player stole the ledger)
He Who Was: A pity. Should I find another murderer in need of torment, I will find you. Until then, farewell.

======== Scenario: sha_mausoleum ========
Session Sequence: PAD_MyrkulSymbol -> PAD_MakeshiftVessel -> PAD_KethericsMap -> PAD_FoundIsobelsPlaque -> PAD_SkullBalthazaarIntro -> PAD_TempleSuspicion -> PAD_FoundDisc_2Players -> PAD_Mural_000 -> PAD_KethericsWifePlaque
----- Session: PAD_MyrkulSymbol -----
Synopsis: Players enter the room where the symbol of Myrkul lies on the floor. Hard religion DC before the PAD plays.

Player: What is that symbol supposed to mean?

----- Session: PAD_MakeshiftVessel -----
Synopsis: Players find a vessel with a half-formed humanoid shape gestating inside and reacts accordingly. The being is just inert flesh and cannot speak.

Player: What is that? Almost looks like someone was trying to grow a person.

----- Session: PAD_KethericsMap -----
Synopsis: Players find the map Ketheric had inside the mausoleum. It shows  the entrance to the Shar Temple (behind Isobel's tomb) and has notes on an attack.

Player: Looks like there's a temple under this place - and something deadly sealed inside it.

----- Session: PAD_FoundIsobelsPlaque -----
Synopsis: PAD for characters reacting to finding Isobels plaque in the Ketheric Mausoleum. Has 3 reaction states:- Already know Ketheric is Isobel's Father- Don't know aboutfamily relationship but have met Isobel- Don't know about family relationship and haven't met Isobel

Player: Isobel. That's the name of the cleric at Last Light Inn, right?
Player: Can she possibly be Ketheric's daughter?

----- Session: PAD_SkullBalthazaarIntro -----
Synopsis: Party reacts to a magic-mouth skull that projects Balthazar's voice, warning them to leave.

Player: Balthazar, a necromancer lap dog of Ketheric Thorm's.
Player: Who knows what he may have up his rotten sleeve.
Player: We need to stay alert.

----- Session: PAD_TempleSuspicion -----
Synopsis: Shadowheart comments on her suspicions that there is probably to the crypt than just a mausoleum. Hinting at the existence of the temple.

Shadowheart: There has to be more to this place. There has to be a reason I came to be here. || [context] NodeContext: Strong suspcion that she's somewhere important for her. Arc: SH is loyal to Shar.

----- Session: PAD_FoundDisc_2Players -----
Synopsis: Players find the disc at the mausoleum that leads to the Shar temple.

Player: That disc looks like it can move - a way forward?
Player: Where will it bring us, though?

----- Session: PAD_Mural_000 -----
Synopsis: Player interacts with the first mural of the Mausoleum puzzle and get the first piece of the story. This mural depicts Moonrise Towers in its heyday, before it turned to darkness. The player's comment varies, depending on whether they've been to MRT or not.

Narrator: *Moonrise Towers. It makes the Urge hiss within. It was part of your disgrace, but how?*<br>

----- Session: PAD_KethericsWifePlaque -----
Synopsis: Reaction from player/narrator who interacts with the tomb of Isobel's mother (and Ketheric's wife).

Narrator: *Here lies Melodia Thorm, beloved wife and mother. Ai armiel telere maenen hir.* || [context] NodeContext: Ah-less-ia /  Ay Army-el Teller-eh Man-en here

If they killed the justiciar, Raphael will appear and negotiate with Yurgir. If the player spared the justiciar, they can confront and fight Yurgir.

Synopsis: The player notices one of the Trial Gems and points it out. If the player knows that the altar requires the gems, they will reiterate the gem's use. Reactivity for finding additional gems subsequently.

Player: A gem. Looks like it might fit in the altar from before.<br> || [context] NodeContext: Karlach note: open to interpretation (to mean 'hey, I spotted it!)  but inspired by jimmy durante

----- Session: PAD_PathOfDarknessHint -----
Synopsis: The player comments after possibly figuring out a clue to successfully completing one of the trials in the Temple of Shar. They must safely cross the room while remembering where the platforms along the way are.

Player: This must be what that book meant. I need to get across - and that means remembering where these platforms are.

----- Session: PAD_MentalTortureHint -----
Synopsis: The player comments after entering one of the trial areas in the temple of Shar. If they read a book in the library before, they'll repeat a hint contained in it about how to complete the trial (defeat their double). Otherwise they'll plead ignorance.

Player: The book was clear - I need to fight myself if I'm to pass this trial.

----- Session: PAD_PathOfDarknessSecondWarning -----
Synopsis: Shar warns player that they only have one attempt left.

: Disappointing. Succeed or fail, the next attempt shall be the last. || [context] NodeContext: Disappointed

----- Session: PAD_HaveAllGems -----
Synopsis: Shadowheart reveals her anticipation and her eagerness to proceed once all trial gems have been collected to open the way to Nightsong.

Shadowheart: That's the last one. The inner sanctum is within reach now.

======== Scenario: sha_necromancer ========
Session Sequence: PAD_MintharaReaction -> AD_EnemyVulnerable -> AD_StartTurn -> AD_GolemDead -> Chosen -> AD_Death -> Barricade -> AD_Justiciar_CombatStarts -> AD_OutsideRoom -> FleshGolem -> AD_DominateGolem -> AD_GhoulSnarl -> AD_Justiciar_TakingTurn_2 -> AD_OrderingGhouls -> GolemInvitation -> AD_BarricadeLeader
----- Session: PAD_MintharaReaction -----
Synopsis: When dialogue with Balthazar ends (or his projection that delivers the narrative bit) this PAD is played by Minthara in party.

Nightwarden Minthara: I wish I could kill that bloated sack of offal, but he may yet help us reach Ketheric.

----- Session: AD_EnemyVulnerable -----
Synopsis: Balthazar orders his flesh golem to attack his enemy while they're vulnerable

Balthazar: We have the upper hand - do your work, Flesh!

----- Session: AD_StartTurn -----
Synopsis: Balthazar gloats at and taunts the player before acting during his turn

Balthazar: It will be a kindness to put an end to your follies.

----- Session: AD_GolemDead -----
Synopsis: Balthazar is angry at his flesh golem being killed

Balthazar: Wretch. You broke my brother!

----- Session: Chosen -----
Synopsis: The player meets Balthazar, the necromancer, in his temporary command centre in the Shar temple. They find him at an altar, repairing one of his damaged undead, while other minions bustle around. Balthazar has been sent by Ketheric Thorm to recover Nightsong, but has been unable to clear a path to her vault. He decides to recruit the player, upon recognising them as tadpoled. The player can agree or decline, and can possibly persuade him to loan his flesh golem to aid their exploration.

Balthazar: I said you'd be back. Reconsidered my proposition?
Player: No, I just decided to kill you instead.
Balthazar: Kill me? Death is my ally, fool.

----- Session: AD_Death -----
Synopsis: Balthazar's final words as he dies

Balthazar: Death... But a fleeting inconvenience.

----- Session: Barricade -----
Synopsis: The player is challenged by some skeleton warriors at a barricade outside the Necromancer's lair. A mindmeld convinces the necromancer to command his skeletons to grant entry. The scene ends with combat with the skeletons, or a shadowquake triggering a fight between player (+ skeletons) against sharran wraiths. Afterwards, the player is invited into Balthazar's inner sanctum.

Reconstituted Duellist: You prowl my battleground - why? Are you friend? Foe? Thieving scavenger?
Narrator: *You find yourself in a dead, putrid skull - somehow hosting a tadpole amongst a squirm of maggots. Another presence lurks within, manipulating the corpse like a puppet.* || [context] CinematicNodeContext: Mindmeld FX. The player winces at the pain of a mindmeld. The skeleton has no visible reaction.
Reconstituted Duellist: Ah. A friend - an uninvited friend. I did not request help.
Reconstituted Duellist: Who am I really speaking to?
Reconstituted Duellist: Come join me and find out. I want to look at you with my own eyes.

======== Scenario: twn_finale ========
Session Sequence: LeavingAct
----- Session: LeavingAct -----
Synopsis: Scene of players leaving SCL to travel to Intermezzo. This scene triggers when the party leave Moonrise Tower after defeating Ketheric. There are two variants. One where the curse has been lifted, one where the curse hasn't been lifted.If the curse has been lifted, Halsin and/or Art Cullagh will be present at Moonrise if alive, and will tell players that the quest has succeeded, and that when they leave Moonrise, they'll see the restults. They tell you to wrap up your business here first. This happens in the dialogues for those characters, not here.If the curse hasn't been lifted, players see a vista of the shadow-cursed lands on leaving Moonrise, and move on toward the Risen Road.

Narrator: *The curse has been lifted, the lands cleansed of the shadows. Ketheric's reign of living death is over.* || [context] CinematicNodeContext: Players leave SCL by the Risen Road. They look back to see beams of light breaking through the clouds.-The curse has been lifted. The clouds above part, and a powerful beam of moonlight shines through and illuminates the town centre where the statue of Ketheric stood. It is now shattered.
Narrator: *Your courage has been tested, and in this, at least, you have triumphed.* || [context] CinematicNodeContext: Cut to close up of the shattered statue. An enormous silver tree bursts through the ground where the statue once stood, silver leaves/fruits sprouting, and the light from above intensifies as the shadows disperse.
[desc] CinematicNodeContext: Cut back to party, with Halsin in shot, looking across the rejuvenating region. Halsin takes front and centre, looking back across the 'healed'vista, overjoyed, and then the party turn and continue their journey || [context] CinematicNodeContext: Cut back to party, with Halsin in shot, looking across the rejuvenating region. ----- Session: ResearchNotes -----
Synopsis: Research notes of the Brewer.He experimented with different poisons on different creatures, trying to figure out the most effective ways of poisoning them. This book also contains info about his attempts to create a Purple Worm Poison.

Narrator: *Research notes. They describe a powerful venom extracted from a rare purple worm. Distiller Thisobald Thorm sought to create a fatal poison using the worm's gullet.*
Narrator: *He procured several parts of a gullet, but rinsed one in error. The poison he brewed was noxious - but not fatal.*
Narrator: *He devoted months to formulating a deadly poison with the remaining ingredients, without success.*
Narrator: *After exhaustive experimentation, he was able to make a near-deadly extract from the glands. But to complete his poison, Thisobald required one last ingredient:*
Narrator: *The petals of a corpse rose.*
Narrator: *The book's index reveals corpse roses may grow near tombs, mausoleums, and particularly redolent cadavers.*
Narrator: *Thisobald enlisted a courier from Baldur's Gate to obtain corpse rose petals and other ingredients and deliver them to a covert location.*
Narrator: *Unfortunately, a deep purple stain darkens the final page, obscuring the parcel's destination.*
Player: Focus your eyes on the page. Mentally separate the blank ink from the purple stain.
: True
Narrator: *Your mind separates the black from the blue, revealing the stash's location. You mark your map as a reminder.*
Narrator: *With the corpse rose petals the package contains, you might create Thisobald's purple worm poison.*
